# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
5 Possible numbers that are less than 6, we only need to choose 4 of them ^T7OceiVx

Since we are going 'along the branch', this is multiplication principle
 ^R4EE5vEo

We could do Pr(one ace)+Pr(two aces) etc...
OR 
We could to the probability of no aces and then subtract using 
Pr(A) = 1-(Pr(A'))

 ^uUbZ0zs5
